border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">但就像你和你的同事一样，它们很乐意接受短期的小小不平等，只要长期来看还是能扯平就好。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></em></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">This</span></em><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> economi<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">c c</span></span>onnection between fairness<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> an<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span></em>cooperation make<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s s</span></span>ense <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to</em> me <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">as</em> <span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">an e</span></span>volutionary biologist.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">在我这个进化生物学家看来，公平和合作之间的经济关联性是合理的。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Afte<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r all</span></span>, your ancestors didn't ge<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t to pass on</span></span><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> their </em>genes because they di<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> we<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ll in</span></span> <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">some</em> absolu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">te </span></span>sense, bu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> because<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> they </em>di<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> better than others.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">毕竟，你的祖先能把他们的基因传下来，并不是因为他们做到了绝对的</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">“</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">好</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">，而是因为他们做得比其他人好。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">We don<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">'t</span></span> ca<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ll it</span></span> surviva<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">l of</span></span><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> the </em>fit, we ca<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ll it</span></span> surviva<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">l of</span></span> <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">the</em> fittest.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">这不叫</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">“</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">适者生存</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">，而是叫</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">“</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">最适者生存</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">As in</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> more fit tha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n o</span></span>thers. It's all relative. OK. So my capuchins don'<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> like <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">it</em> when <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">they </em>ge<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> less tha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n a</span></span>nother.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">也就是说，要比别人更会适应。全都是相对的。好。所以我的卷尾猴不喜欢拿到比其他猴子差的东西。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">An<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> they're perfectly happy <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to </em>sacrifice their cucumbers<em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> to </em><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">level</strong><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"> the </em>playing field. That's great.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">它们非常愿意牺牲它们的小黄瓜来让情况变公平。那很棒。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">But what we would ca<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ll a</span></span> sens<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e of f</span></span>airne<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ss in </span></span><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"></em>humans also means tha<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> we care when we ge<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> more than someone else.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">但当我们说人类有公平感，也表示我们会在乎自己拿得比别人多。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Wha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t a</span></span>bou<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> my monkeys? <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">It </em><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">turns ou<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span></strong> <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">that</em> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">primates</strong> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">do</strong> notice when they ge<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> more tha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n o</span></span>ther<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s, o</span></span>r a<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> least some <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">of </em>them do. My capuchins do not.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我的猴子会吗？结果发现，灵长类动物确实会注意到自己得到的比较多，至少有些灵长类动物会。我的卷尾猴不会。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">AT first Shasta could see nothing in the valley below him but a sea of mist with a few domes and pinnacles rising from it; but as the light increased and the mist cleared away he saw more and more. A broad river divided itself into two streams and on the island between them stood the city of Tashbaan, one of the wonders of the world. Round the very edge of the island, so that the water lapped against the stone, ran high walls strengthened with so many towers that he soon gave up trying to count them.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">起初，沙斯塔看不清下面山谷里的景物，但用个雾霭的海洋，从中矗出些圆屋顶和小尖塔，但光芒增强、雾霭廓清时，他看到的景物就越来越多了。一条宽阔的大河分成两条支流，支流之间的岛上耸立着塔什班城——世界上有名的奇观之一。环绕着岛屿的四周，筑有一系列高大的城墙，中间夹着许多堡垒塔楼，以资拱卫。流水拍打着石头城。堡垒又那么多，沙斯塔不久就不想去一一点清数目了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我是M公司的玛丽。我打电话告诉你你被录用了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 太好了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我们欢迎你来为公司工作。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 你想让我什么时候开始工作？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 越快越好。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我至少需要2周。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 好的，你接受这个职位吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 接受。为你们工作是种荣幸。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Mike, This is Mary from M. I’m calling to offer you the position you interviewed for.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Great.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: We would love to have you come to work for us.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: When do you want me start?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: As soon as possible.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I need at least two weeks.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: OK. Do you accept the offer?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes, it would be an honor to work for you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">On second thought, I'm going home on this vacation.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">_______________，我打算回家休假。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">仔细想了之后</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;text-align: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. 向工人们定下规则</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. 她不肯听从任何人的指挥。</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p></p></section><section style="margin-top: 0.3em;padding-bottom: 1em;background-color: rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.44);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-width: 0.2em;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(151, 195, 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Scars remind us where we've been. They don't have to dictate where we're going.</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. been和going 在句中形成对比强调，均需重读；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. dictate作动词时一般重音在后/dɪkˈteɪt/；作名词时重音在前/ˈdɪkteɪt/。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：remind XX what/when/where/how...</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">提醒某人（什么/何时/哪里/如何）...</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I need the notes to <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">remind </strong></em></span><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong>me what to say</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我需要这些笔记来<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">提醒</strong>我该说什么。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Its only purpose is to <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">remind </strong></em></span><strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em>you where you started</em></span></strong>. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">它唯一的目的是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">提醒</strong>你，你是从哪里起步的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. dictate verb. 支配，影响，决定</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">近义词：determine</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-linktype="2" href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653548556&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=f3fffa7e734bf7a7ea056282666310e6&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="点击链接跳转回顾【dictate &amp; dictator】">点击链接跳转回顾【dictate &amp; dictator】</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：dictate what/how/where etc.</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Funds <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">dictate </strong></em></span>what we can do.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">资金的多少<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">决定</strong>我们能做些什么。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's generally your job that <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">dictates </strong></em></span>where you live now.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一般说来，你住在什么地方是由你的工作<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">决定</strong>的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句</strong></span>：The company you keep is going to kind of <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">dictate </strong></em></span>where you go in life.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你的同伴/伴侣会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">决定</strong>你的人生走向。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句</strong></span>：Those fundamentals <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">dictate </strong></em></span>where you're going.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这些基本原则<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">决定</strong>了你的方向。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The unsub could be letting his emotions <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">dictate </strong></em></span>his actions.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">嫌犯任由自己的情绪<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">操控</strong>行为。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">*dictate的其他用法：</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">① “强加某事物于某人”：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">dictate sth to sb</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">dictate </strong></em></span>rules to the workers</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">向工人们定<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">下规则</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">② “指挥”、“摆布”：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She refused to <span style="text-decoration: underline;">be <span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">dictated </strong></em></span>to</span> by anyone.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她不肯听从任何人的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">指挥</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">③ 由于dictate有“（不容分说地）决定”的意思，所以也可以用来表示“大权在握，说一不二”。因此，派生的名词dictator就是“独裁者”，dictatorship就是“独裁”或“专政”。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);padding: 0px 9px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">请用 <strong border-box;">不要<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">过度使用</span>头发定型产品。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 60%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.625" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKeDPdicpofjqJEHVib9j3gJpowmLjp9u56QXX9S1cEDDDfibibL64MwE7REyxZ59p4fxCfv4CHeGQjlvg/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="800" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">cologne /kəˈləʊn $ -ˈloʊn/ n. 科隆香水，古龙水</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇小故事：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;padding: 10px;background-color: rgba(222, 237, 242, 0.89);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: 14%;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0% 5px;line-height: 0.8;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(107, 160, 172);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;line-height: 0.8;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 0.8em solid rgb(107, 160, 172);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: 78%;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(107, 160, 172);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">向上滑动阅览</p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">cologne（古龙水）：诞生古龙水的德国城市科隆</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在18世纪的德国城市科隆（Cologne），有一位名叫吉欧凡尼•玛丽亚•法利纳（Giovanni Maria Farina）的意大利理发匠。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他的理发店生意十分火爆，因为他不仅擅长理发，更重要的时，他家有一个祖传秘方，可以用来调制一种特别的盥洗用水。用这种盥洗用水洗头和脸后，令人神清气爽，还留有一种淡淡的香味。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">法利纳的盥洗用水在整个科隆城都出了名，顾客们络绎不绝。甚至有一位顾客特意登门拜访，希望购买一些这种盥洗用水，因为他第二天需要出席一个重要场合，希望用法利纳的盥洗用水来帮助自己显得更加精神。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">受此触动，法利纳先生找到了另一条致富途径。从此以后，他致力于生产这种盥洗用水，并与1709年正式推向市场。由于这种盥洗用水最早问世于科隆市，人们便将其称为“科隆水”，后来简称“科隆”（cologne），中文译为“古龙水”。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">欧洲的男士们特别喜欢古龙水的香气，他们喜欢在洗澡后往身上喷洒这种清新爽快价格又不太高的“香水”，因此早期的古龙水被看作是“男用香水”。法国皇帝拿破仑就特别喜欢古龙水，据说每个月要用掉60瓶古龙水。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="background-color: rgba(254, 255, 255, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">perfume  /ˈpɜːfjuːm $ ˈpɜːr-/ n.香水</span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="background-color: rgba(254, 255, 255, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">perfume </span><span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">counter</span> of the store </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">商店的<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">香水柜台</span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 60%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.75" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKeDPdicpofjqJEHVib9j3gJpo0tpmS6ia4UtoDQpGaTt2E37qdxhe6dVgHMYCN2QV2arlEVNxBxzrpjw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="520" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She was <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">wearing too much perfume</span>. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">喷了太多的香水</span>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 60%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1" wouldn't fix.</span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 87);box-sizing: border-box;">过度</span>锻炼。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKeDPdicpofjqJEHVib9j3gJpoic0x4zWAyIIr4KFwzKSrdUBqNbXXYmPibqQraOulic85M8QzE2XZ06KSw/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" border-box;">不要<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">过度使用</span>头发定型产品。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 60%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.625" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKeDPdicpofjqJEHVib9j3gJpowmLjp9u56QXX9S1cEDDDfibibL64MwE7REyxZ59p4fxCfv4CHeGQjlvg/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="800" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">cologne /kəˈləʊn $ -ˈloʊn/ n. 科隆香水，古龙水</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇小故事：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;padding: 10px;background-color: rgba(222, 237, 242, 0.89);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: 14%;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0% 5px;line-height: 0.8;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(107, 160, 172);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;line-height: 0.8;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 0.8em solid rgb(107, 160, 172);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: 78%;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(107, 160, 172);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">向上滑动阅览</p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">cologne（古龙水）：诞生古龙水的德国城市科隆</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在18世纪的德国城市科隆（Cologne），有一位名叫吉欧凡尼•玛丽亚•法利纳（Giovanni Maria Farina）的意大利理发匠。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他的理发店生意十分火爆，因为他不仅擅长理发，更重要的时，他家有一个祖传秘方，可以用来调制一种特别的盥洗用水。用这种盥洗用水洗头和脸后，令人神清气爽，还留有一种淡淡的香味。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">法利纳的盥洗用水在整个科隆城都出了名，顾客们络绎不绝。甚至有一位顾客特意登门拜访，希望购买一些这种盥洗用水，因为他第二天需要出席一个重要场合，希望用法利纳的盥洗用水来帮助自己显得更加精神。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">受此触动，法利纳先生找到了另一条致富途径。从此以后，他致力于生产这种盥洗用水，并与1709年正式推向市场。由于这种盥洗用水最早问世于科隆市，人们便将其称为“科隆水”，后来简称“科隆”（cologne），中文译为“古龙水”。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">欧洲的男士们特别喜欢古龙水的香气，他们喜欢在洗澡后往身上喷洒这种清新爽快价格又不太高的“香水”，因此早期的古龙水被看作是“男用香水”。法国皇帝拿破仑就特别喜欢古龙水，据说每个月要用掉60瓶古龙水。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 60%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6666667" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKeDPdicpofjqJEHVib9j3gJpoznDyiahHXROoRkNNrm7BUASszC1DGib6rVOSkB5n2GA4Pj2WicqbPdZeg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="background-color: rgba(254, 255, 255, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">perfume  /ˈpɜːfjuːm $ ˈpɜːr-/ n.香水</span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="background-color: rgba(254, 255, 255, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">perfume </span><span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">counter</span> of the store </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">商店的<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">香水柜台</span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKeDPdicpofjqJEHVib9j3gJpo0tpmS6ia4UtoDQpGaTt2E37qdxhe6dVgHMYCN2QV2arlEVNxBxzrpjw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="520" border-box;">She was <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">wearing too much perfume</span>. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">喷了太多的香水</span>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: her.</span></strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(210, 239, 230);height: 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="background-color: rgba(254, 255, 255, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">要看你是想吸引她还是想熏死她</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这句话省略了it，</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">it depends  那得看情况</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">‘Your job sounds fun.’ </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">‘<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">It depends what </span>you mean by ‘fun’.’</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“你的工作听起来很有乐趣。”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">这就要看</span>你说的‘乐趣’是什么意思了。”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I shouldn't be too late. But <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">it depends if </span>the traffic's bad.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我应该不会太迟。不过<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">这取决于</span>交通<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">是否</span>拥挤了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I might not go. <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">It depends how</span> tired I am.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我不一定去。<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">这要看</span>我累不累。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 60%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.9327273" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKeDPdicpofjqJEHVib9j3gJpoEPNSyabD5o71SxfuAXrJw6SsH3biaP3dpebkdnrbBjuINnvyPWfZUSg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="550" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">fumigate /ˈfjuːmɪɡeɪt/ v</strong>.<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">〔为消毒、杀菌、杀虫等而用化学品、烟或气〕熏蒸；烟熏</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We had to <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">fumigate</span> the cellar to get rid of cockroaches.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们不得不<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">烟熏</span>地下室来除蟑螂。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Chimpanzee </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">（n.）UK/tʃɪmpæn'ziː/ US/ˌtʃɪmpæn'zi/  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(sometimes called chimps) A chimpanzee is a kind of small African ape. 黑猩猩</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Impressive</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ɪm'presɪv/ US/ɪm'prɛsɪv/(adj.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">making a deep and usually favorable impression on the mind or senses</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">e.g.That's very impressive. Let's see the next one.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">太赞了。我们来看下一个。---《艾伦秀》</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Upset </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ʌp'set/US /ʌp'sɛt/(adj.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">you are unhappy or disappointed because something unpleasant has happened to you. 难过的; 沮丧的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">e.g.Okay, I know you're upset... - I'm not upset.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">好吧 我知道你不开心 -才没有。《马男波杰克第一季》</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Equality </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ɪ'kwɒlɪtɪ/ US/ɪ'kwɑləti/(n.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Equality is the same status, rights, and responsibilities for all the members of a society, group, or family. 平等Inequality UK/ɪnɪ'kwɒlɪtɪ/ US/ˌɪnɪ'kwɑləti/(n.)the difference in social status, wealth, or opportunity between people or groups. 不平等; 不公平</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">e.g.And China also has broad income inequality.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中国还存在广泛的收入不均衡。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Fair </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/feə/ US/fɛr/(adj.) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Something or someone that is fair is reasonable, right, and just. 公平的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">e.g.All right, okay, fair is fair.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">好吧 公平至上。---《瑞克和莫蒂第一季》</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Unfair </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ʌn'feə/ US/'ʌn'fɛr/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">not fair; marked by injustice or partiality or deception不公平的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">e.g.Hey, this is so unfair! -Monica: Oh, why is it unfair?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">－嗨，这太不公平了吧！－为什么不公平？---《老友记 第一季》</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Unfairness</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(n.) -ness.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">e.g.President Obama said many Americans feel deep unfairness with the US criminal justice system.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">奥巴马总统表示，许多美国人深感美国的刑事司法制度不公平。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">survival of the fittest  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a natural process resulting in the evolution of organisms best adapted to the environment适者生存</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Make sense </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be reasonable or logical or comprehensible讲得通，有道理</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">e.g.Well, it made sense. It made perfect sense.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“哎呀，这是很有道理的。完全有道理的。---《万物简史》</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Advantage</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(n.)UK/əd'vɑːntɪdʒ/US/əd'væntɪdʒ/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">An advantage is a way in which one thing is better than another. 优势</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Take advantage of sth./sb.  to use sth./sb. in a selfish way in order to achieve a personal benefit, usually by exploiting a weakness利用某人、某事</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">e.g.You're taking advantage of Mrs Hughes' absence.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">趁Hughes夫人不在就胡来。---《唐顿庄园》</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-disadvantage(n.) at a disadvantage you have a problem or difficulty that many other people do not have, which makes it harder for you to be successful. 处于劣势</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Play fair</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(also fair play)conduct that adheres to the rules or is just and equitable</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 公平的比赛(公平对待)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">e.g.I'm not sure they even play fair to get what they have.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我甚至不确定他们是凭真本事进来的。---《妖女迷行第一季》</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: border-box;">当你拥有的比邻居多，你可能不觉得不公平，但当邻居拥有的比你多时，你就会认为不公平。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: an</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> importan</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> question, though. Why do we care abou</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> inequalit</span><span style="text-decoration: sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">r unfairness when we are the ones who </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(227, 108, 10);box-sizing: border-box;">are</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> unfairly benefiting?</span></p><p style="text-align: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Inside the walls the island rose in a hill and every bit of that hill, up to the Tisroc's palace and the great temple of Tash at the top, was completely covered with buildings - terrace above terrace, street above street, zigzag roads or huge flights of steps bordered with orange trees and lemon trees, roof gardens, balconies, deep archways, pillared colonnades, spires, battlements, minarets, pinnacles. And when at last the sun rose out of the sea and the great silver-plated dome of the temple flashed back its light, he was almost dazzled.   </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">城墙里边，岛屿上降起个小山，山上每一块土地，从山麓直到山顶上蒂斯罗克的王宫和塔什神的庙宇，都布满了建筑物——重重叠叠，台地之上还有台地，街道之上还有街道，曲曲折折的路或是巨大的台阶，两边都种上了橘子树和柠檬树，处处是屋顶花园、阳台、深邃的拱廊、柱廊、塔尖、雉堞墙、寺院尖塔、哥特式建筑的尖顶。太阳终于从海上升起来时，寺院巨大的镀银圆屋顶把阳光反射出来，耀得他眼花缭乱。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我可以和Tom Smith通话吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我就是Tom。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 史密斯先生，我是Marry Zhang。几天前我曾和您面试过，我打电话是来了解下空着的秘书职位的状况。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我们还没做过任何决定。我们已经有几个人选，我们还在仔细选择。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我明白了，我对这个职位很感兴趣。如果你需要其他材料的话请打电话给我。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我会的，谢谢。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Hi, may I speak to Tom Smith?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes, this is Tom.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Mr. Smith, this is Marry Zhang. I interviewed with you a few days ago. I was just calling to follow up on the status of the opening secretary position.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: We haven’t made any decision yet. Although we do have a couple we’re looking at very carefully.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I see, well, I’m very interested in the position and I hope you’ll call if there’s any additional information you need.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I certainly will. Thanks for calling.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">__________________, I forgot it was your birthday last week.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">说实话，我忘了上星期那天是你的生日。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">To tell the truth</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section What is A if not C. = A is nothing but C. = A is C.</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">griefs</strong></em></span>.</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">友谊增进欢乐，分担<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">忧愁</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">grief </strong></em></span>over the destruction of our ship.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">为我们的船被毁而<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">悲伤</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 坚韧不拔的，不屈不挠的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He is a 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">真正的挑战是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">坚持不懈</strong>...</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p </strong></em></span>with difficult students.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对难教的学生你必须<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">坚持</strong>诲人不倦的精神。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: border-box;">persevere</strong></em></span>, trusting in what hopes he has,</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→perseverance n. 毅力; 不屈不挠的精神</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-linktype="2" href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653516871&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=011f0245e8fad74a61fa6de55481f2ed&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="点击链接跳转回顾【perseverance】">点击链接跳转回顾【perseverance】</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. 拓展：</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Love always perseveres. 这句话出自《圣经》。原文节选如下：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"></em></p><blockquote class="js_blockquote_wrap" data-author-name="" data-content-utf8-length="280" data-source-title="圣经" data-type="2" data-url=""><section class="js_blockquote_digest"><section><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">Love does not delight in evil but rejoices with the truth.</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">It always protects, always trusts, always hopes, always perseveres.</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">爱不喜欢不义，只喜欢真理。爱是凡事包容，凡事相信，凡事盼望，凡事忍耐。</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"></em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">影片中之所以Wanda有被这句话安慰到，因为Wanda失去亲人，悲伤排山倒海而来，几乎将她压垮，她不知道如何面对承受这种情感。这句话告诉了她，悲痛并不是件坏事，悲痛甚至可以来得更深或者更久都无所谓，因为为亲人悲痛，也是把爱延续下去的方式。</em></p></section></section><section class="blockquote_info translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;padding: 10px;background-color: rgba(222, 237, 242, 0.89);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: 14%;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0% 5px;line-height: 0.8;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(107, 160, 172);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;line-height: 0.8;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 0.8em solid rgb(107, 160, 172);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: 78%;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(107, 160, 172);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">向上滑动阅览</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">【bloody 拓展小知识】</p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们知道blood表示血。那bloody为什么会是一个加强语气的词汇呢？</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">bloody 古英语作blodig，一般也只是单纯地将它视为blood（血）的派生词，blood加后缀-y所构成。但若追溯一下其历史，我们就会发现这是个与众不同的词。英语词典编纂者帕特里奇（Eric Partidge, 1894-1979）曾撰文对bloody作了专门论述，该文长达2000字。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">从18世纪初以来很长一段时间内，bloody用来加强语气，表示“很”或“非常”的含义时，在英国一直被列为禁忌语。萧伯纳的名剧《卖花女》（Pygmalion）仅因剧中用了bloody一词，1912年在伦敦首演时竟然引起巨大轰动。据报道，当女主角卖花女Liza说出“Not bloody likely”（不大可能）一语，全场观众无不震惊。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在出现该语的一幕戏中，观众发现自己很难把注意力集中到剧情上，而是全神贯注地等待着那句令人惊愕的话吐自一位女士之口。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英国人之所以不愿说出或不愿听到bloody一词，是因为有人往往把它与menstruation（月经）相联系，也有人往往把它与Christ's blood（天哪）或由God's blood缩略而成的诅咒语'sblood（该死）等相联系，还有人认为它来自by our Lady（圣母啊）一语。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">最简单的解释是，许多人怕血，长期以来血一直是暴力和死亡的象征。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">不管怎么说，bloody会使人产生污秽、亵渎等不好的联想。然而bloody在美国英语中则一向是个无关痛痒的词。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">随着时间的推移，如今英国人虽然对bloody已不那么忌讳了，但是有身份的人在某些场合（如男女都在的场合）仍然避而不用。</span></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 8%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一起看看文中其他实用表达~</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0% border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style='font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", show a bit of respect!</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style='font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;'>为了供养你，你父亲</span><span style='font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;'>拼命工作</span><span style='font-family: style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;padding: 10px;background-color: rgba(222, 237, 242, 0.89);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: 14%;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0% 5px;line-height: 0.8;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(107, 160, 172);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;line-height: 0.8;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 0.8em solid rgb(107, 160, 172);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: 78%;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(107, 160, 172);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">向上滑动阅览</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">【bloody 拓展小知识】</p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们知道blood表示血。那bloody为什么会是一个加强语气的词汇呢？</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">bloody 古英语作blodig，一般也只是单纯地将它视为blood（血）的派生词，blood加后缀-y所构成。但若追溯一下其历史，我们就会发现这是个与众不同的词。英语词典编纂者帕特里奇（Eric Partidge, 1894-1979）曾撰文对bloody作了专门论述，该文长达2000字。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">从18世纪初以来很长一段时间内，bloody用来加强语气，表示“很”或“非常”的含义时，在英国一直被列为禁忌语。萧伯纳的名剧《卖花女》（Pygmalion）仅因剧中用了bloody一词，1912年在伦敦首演时竟然引起巨大轰动。据报道，当女主角卖花女Liza说出“Not bloody likely”（不大可能）一语，全场观众无不震惊。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在出现该语的一幕戏中，观众发现自己很难把注意力集中到剧情上，而是全神贯注地等待着那句令人惊愕的话吐自一位女士之口。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英国人之所以不愿说出或不愿听到bloody一词，是因为有人往往把它与menstruation（月经）相联系，也有人往往把它与Christ's blood（天哪）或由God's blood缩略而成的诅咒语'sblood（该死）等相联系，还有人认为它来自by our Lady（圣母啊）一语。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">最简单的解释是，许多人怕血，长期以来血一直是暴力和死亡的象征。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">不管怎么说，bloody会使人产生污秽、亵渎等不好的联想。然而bloody在美国英语中则一向是个无关痛痒的词。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">随着时间的推移，如今英国人虽然对bloody已不那么忌讳了，但是有身份的人在某些场合（如男女都在的场合）仍然避而不用。</span></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 8%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 50%;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.144578313253012" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/FCxBvbuaS5ODMOjlrZSBKawErV58QxAxDtibFSJbibtPaWHQASVCj2GmyK0Zwibb6Trut3zF2ThMk0OLUjibIQR5tA/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="83" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 92%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 12px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="color: rgb(43, 110, 198);font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="background-color: rgba(254, 255, 255, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"> </strong><strong style="background-color: rgba(254, 255, 255, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">“...不得了” 还可以怎样说</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0% 16px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;color: rgb(109, 109, 109);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 1px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;padding: 0px 31px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style='font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(210, 239, 230);height: 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你到底为什么要拉我出来？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">what/why/how etc on earth ...? </strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">究竟，到底〔用于询问令人惊讶或生气的事〕</strong></p><p style="white-space: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你那么做<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">究竟为了什么</span>？</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align:
