0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">occasional</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adjective   /əˈkeɪ.ʒən.əl/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：not happening or done often or regularly偶尔的；不经常的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I play the occasional game of tennis.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我偶尔打打网球。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Occasion  /əˈkeɪ.ʒən/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：a particular time, especially when something happens or has happened（尤指某事发生的）时刻，时候</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We met on several occasions to discuss the issue.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们几次会面讨论这个问题。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：a special or formal event特殊场合；重大活动；盛会</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sara's party was quite an occasion - there were over a hundred people </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">there.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">萨拉的聚会真是一次盛会——有一百多人参加。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：an opportunity or reason for doing something or for something to happen时机，机会；原因，理由</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The 200th anniversary of Mozart's death was the occasion for hundreds of special films, books and concerts.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">为纪念莫扎特逝世200周年，出现了数以百计的专题电影、书籍及音乐会。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：on occasion sometimes, but not often有时；偶尔，间或</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He has, on occasion, made a small mistake.他有时犯点小错误。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">verb </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to cause something造成，引起；惹起</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Her refusal occasioned a lot of trouble.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她的拒绝引出许多麻烦。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">occasionally</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adverb   /əˈkeɪ.ʒən.əl.i/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：sometimes but not often偶尔，间或；有时</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I see him occasionally in town.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">incredibly</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adverb   /ɪnˈkred.ə.bli/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：used for saying that something is very difficult to believe难以置信地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Incredibly, no one was hurt in the accident.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">事故中居然没有人受伤，这真是令人难以置信。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：extremely极其</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He was incredibly rich.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他极其富有。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">interconnected</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adjective    /ˌɪn.t̬ɚ.kəˈnek.tɪd/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：with different parts or things connected or related to each other互相连接的；互相联系的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The new home consists of seven interconnected buildings.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">新的家由七栋相互连接的建筑组成。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">interdependent</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adjective  /ˌɪn.t̬ɚ.dɪˈpen.dənt/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 英文释义：depending on each other互相依赖的，互相依存的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All living things are interdependent.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所有的生物都是互相依存的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">cognitive</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adjective  /ˈkɑːɡ.nə.t̬ɪv/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：connected with thinking or conscious mental processes感知的；认知的；认识力的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Some of her cognitive functions have been impaired.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她的部分认知能力受到了损害。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">underplay</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">verb /ˌʌn.dɚˈpleɪ/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 英文释义：to make something such as a dangerous situation seem less important or dangerous than it really is低调处理；对…轻描淡写；贬低…的重要性</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">While not wanting to underplay the seriousness of the situation, I have to say that it is not as bad as people seem to think.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">尽管我并不想低估形势的严重性，但还是不得不说事情并不像人们想象的那么糟糕。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">sheer</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adjective   /ʃɪr/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：used to emphasize how very great, important, or powerful a</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">quality or feeling is; nothing except完全的，彻底的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The suggestion is sheer nonsense.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个建议纯粹是胡言乱语。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">ubiquity</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun  /juːˈbɪk.wə.t̬i/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 英文释义：the fact that something or someone seems to be everywhere（人或物）无处不在，普遍存在</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the ubiquity of fast-food outlets   快餐店的无处不在</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">magnitude</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun  /ˈmæɡ.nə.tuːd/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 英文释义：the large size or importance of something巨大；重大，重要性</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They don't seem to grasp the magnitude of the problem.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们似乎未领会问题的重要性。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">in other words</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：used to introduce an explanation that is simpler than the one given earlier换句话说，换言之</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He was economical with the truth - in other words, he was lying.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他没讲多少实话——换言之，他在撒谎。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">literally</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adverb  /ˈlɪt̬.ɚ.əl.i/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：using the real or original meaning of a word or phrase确实地；名副其实地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They were responsible for literally millions of deaths.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们的确对数百万人的死负有责任。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：If you translate literally, you translate each word in a text separately, without looking at how the words are used together in a phrase or sentence. 逐字（翻译）地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Translations that are done too literally often don't flow well or don't </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">sound natural.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">太拘泥于字面意思的翻译往往会不太流畅或不太自然。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：used to emphasize what you are saying（用于强调所说的话）确实，真正地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He missed that kick literally by miles.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他那一脚踢丢得确实相差好几英里远。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：simply or just只是，仅仅，就</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Then you literally cut the sausage down the middle.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那么你就从香肠的中间切开吧。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">fall apart</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to break into pieces破碎；散架</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My poor old boots are falling apart.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我可怜的旧靴子快散架了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：If an organization, system, or agreement falls apart, it fails or stops working effectively.破裂；解体，瓦解</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The deal fell apart because of a lack of financing.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">由于缺乏资金，这笔交易告吹了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to experience serious emotional problems that make you unable to think or act in the usual way（感情）崩溃，垮掉</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">After his wife died, he began to fall apart.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">妻子过世后，他精神开始垮掉。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;padding: 3px 10px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: 0px 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="padding-bottom: 8px;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="clear: none;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读</span></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(206, 169, 203);padding: 10px;box-shadow: rgb(204, 204, 204) 2.6px 2.6px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">Friday</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="line-height: 19px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The river banks on each side of the valley were such a mass of gardens that they looked at first like forest, until you got closer and saw the white walls of innumerable houses peeping out from beneath the trees. Soon after that, Shasta noticed a delicious smell of flowers and fruit. About fifteen minutes later they were down among them, plodding on a level road with white walls on each side and trees bending over the walls. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">山谷两边河岸上花园那么多，乍看简直就像个森林，直至走近了，看到树木下露出无数房屋的雪白墙垣，才明白了真相。不久以后，沙斯塔便觉得有阵阵芬芳的花果香气。大约十五分钟以后他们便到了花园之间，他们走在一条平坦的道路上，两边都是雪白的墙垣，下垂的花木枝条伸出墙来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 哈利好沮丧，不和任何人说话。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我很能知道那种感受。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你什么意思？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 去年我被解雇时我也很沮丧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Harry is so down that he won't talk to anyone.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I know only too well what that's like.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What do you mean?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I was very sad when I was laid off last year.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">_________________, one should be dressed neatly when being interviewed for a job.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">不用说，参加面试时应该穿上正式的衣服。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Needless to say</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: 16px;"><section
